üá∫üá∏ IMPORTANT!

An important announcement for everyone who purchased an NFT token to receive a Freeland passport on the OpenSea platform. The GrandBazar platform will be connected later. As we reported earlier, in order to get a physical copy of the passport, you need to pass KYC. To do this, we have created a special form that determines the presence of a token in the user's wallet (link under the post).

In order to fill out the form, you need to log in using Metamask in the Polygon network.

After sending the data for further consideration, upon completion of filling out the form, it will be necessary to burn üî• your existing token (a special burning button will appear). To do this, you need a minimum amount of Polygon MATIC tokens on your wallet (literally 2-3 cents with gas). After burning, a new registration token is sent to the user's wallet, which stores the status of your Freeland document, including the validity of the document.

As soon as the physical copy of your passport is ready, we will contact you by email and request an address to send your document (by DHL or similar). And you can officially be considered a citizen of the virtual state of Freeland, located on the territory of the digital space! üöÄ

Disciplinary action taken against faulty relayer

During the liquidity migration protocol for the Bridge DAO, one of the relayers from the Korean community carried out an attack on the network by selling vesting tokens to destabilize the network.

The relayer was reported to the DAO by the Korean community, and in accordance with DAO protocols, their tokens have been slashed and their WTON tokens have been blocked until the DAO finishes investigating.

For full details on the event and disciplinary measures, read our report on Medium
